As a nod to Jordan's on-court play, the Men's Air Jordan Retro 5 Basketball Shoes were designed to look like a fighter plane. In the famed model, MJ earned his fourth consecutive scoring title, sixth All-Star appearance and led the Bulls to the Eastern Conference Finals.
